## <span id="SafeMath"></span> `SafeMath`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-]
- [`div(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-]
- [`sub(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-]
- [`add(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-]
- [`mod(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mul(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-"></span> `div(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-"></span> `sub(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-"></span> `add(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mod(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="SafeMath8"></span> `SafeMath8`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-]
- [`div(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-]
- [`sub(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-]
- [`add(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-]
- [`mod(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-]
### <span id="SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mul(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-"></span> `div(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-"></span> `sub(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-"></span> `add(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mod(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.

This Library is part of many that Ice uses form a robust File Management System

## <span id="SafeMath"></span> `SafeMath`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-]
- [`div(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-]
- [`sub(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-]
- [`add(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-]
- [`mod(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mul(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-"></span> `div(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-"></span> `sub(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-"></span> `add(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mod(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="SafeMath8"></span> `SafeMath8`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-]
- [`div(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-]
- [`sub(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-]
- [`add(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-]
- [`mod(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-]
### <span id="SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mul(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-"></span> `div(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-"></span> `sub(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-"></span> `add(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mod(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.

## <span id="SafeMath"></span> `SafeMath`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-]
- [`div(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-]
- [`sub(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-]
- [`add(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-]
- [`mod(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mul(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-"></span> `div(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-"></span> `sub(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-"></span> `add(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mod(uint256 a, uint256 b) → uint256` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="SafeMath16"></span> `SafeMath16`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint16 a, uint16 b)`][SafeMath16-mul-uint16-uint16-]
- [`div(uint16 a, uint16 b)`][SafeMath16-div-uint16-uint16-]
- [`sub(uint16 a, uint16 b)`][SafeMath16-sub-uint16-uint16-]
- [`add(uint16 a, uint16 b)`][SafeMath16-add-uint16-uint16-]
- [`mod(uint16 a, uint16 b)`][SafeMath16-mod-uint16-uint16-]
### <span id="SafeMath16-mul-uint16-uint16-"></span> `mul(uint16 a, uint16 b) → uint16` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath16-div-uint16-uint16-"></span> `div(uint16 a, uint16 b) → uint16` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath16-sub-uint16-uint16-"></span> `sub(uint16 a, uint16 b) → uint16` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath16-add-uint16-uint16-"></span> `add(uint16 a, uint16 b) → uint16` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath16-mod-uint16-uint16-"></span> `mod(uint16 a, uint16 b) → uint16` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="SafeMath32"></span> `SafeMath32`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint32 a, uint32 b)`][SafeMath32-mul-uint32-uint32-]
- [`div(uint32 a, uint32 b)`][SafeMath32-div-uint32-uint32-]
- [`sub(uint32 a, uint32 b)`][SafeMath32-sub-uint32-uint32-]
- [`add(uint32 a, uint32 b)`][SafeMath32-add-uint32-uint32-]
- [`mod(uint32 a, uint32 b)`][SafeMath32-mod-uint32-uint32-]
### <span id="SafeMath32-mul-uint32-uint32-"></span> `mul(uint32 a, uint32 b) → uint32` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath32-div-uint32-uint32-"></span> `div(uint32 a, uint32 b) → uint32` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath32-sub-uint32-uint32-"></span> `sub(uint32 a, uint32 b) → uint32` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath32-add-uint32-uint32-"></span> `add(uint32 a, uint32 b) → uint32` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath32-mod-uint32-uint32-"></span> `mod(uint32 a, uint32 b) → uint32` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="SafeMath8"></span> `SafeMath8`

Math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-]
- [`div(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-]
- [`sub(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-]
- [`add(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-]
- [`mod(uint8 a, uint8 b)`][SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-]
### <span id="SafeMath8-mul-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mul(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Multiplies two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-div-uint8-uint8-"></span> `div(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Integer division of two numbers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.

### <span id="SafeMath8-sub-uint8-uint8-"></span> `sub(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Subtracts two numbers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).

### <span id="SafeMath8-add-uint8-uint8-"></span> `add(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Adds two numbers, reverts on overflow.

### <span id="SafeMath8-mod-uint8-uint8-"></span> `mod(uint8 a, uint8 b) → uint8` (internal)

Divides two numbers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),
reverts when dividing by zero.



## <span id="Ownable"></span> `Ownable`

The Ownable contract has an owner address, and provides basic authorization control
functions, this simplifies the implementation of "user permissions".

- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`constructor()`][Ownable-constructor--]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`][Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-]
### <span id="Ownable-onlyOwner--"></span> `onlyOwner()`

Throws if called by any account other than the owner.

### <span id="Ownable-constructor--"></span> `constructor()` (public)

The Ownable constructor sets the original `owner` of the contract to the sender
account.

### <span id="Ownable-owner--"></span> `owner() → address` (public)



### <span id="Ownable-isOwner--"></span> `isOwner() → bool` (public)



### <span id="Ownable-renounceOwnership--"></span> `renounceOwnership()` (public)

Allows the current owner to relinquish control of the contract.


### <span id="Ownable-transferOwnership-address-"></span> `transferOwnership(address newOwner)` (public)

Allows the current owner to transfer control of the contract to a newOwner.


### <span id="Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-"></span> `_transferOwnership(address newOwner)` (internal)

Transfers control of the contract to a newOwner.


### <span id="Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-"></span> `OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`
